Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time an abscess came in the armpit, and swelled so much that it burst, and began to putrefy.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the treatment, and I thought for a long time, but could not stop the wound from bleeding.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong dressing, and out came a bone, then after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I make the wound, and press bones until the woman is in a better position.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and keep the woman long time in this manner, and then a little more of the bone at the joint.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not found this chapter except that, when the master finds an unusual thing, he knows what to do about it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the wife to her place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here comes the translation for the next sentence:
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	"Furthermore, the horns should be more delicate than the restrictor, and made from ebony or boxwood;"
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	"and the mouth of the tube should be one finger wide, and the trees (?) one finger thick, and half a palm in length;"
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	"and between the two links should be two joints of this same tube, which are closed at both ends, half a palm in length or slightly more;"
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	And this second alignment is placed in the mouth of the patient to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more delicate and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, resembling pliers.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	And have two alignments for each joint, as you see, one palm in length and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	And when you see opening the anus with all the instruments, make her sit on a chair, feet apart and legs open,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	Then place the two instruments side by side in the anus, and hold the handle of the instrument under her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instruments, as you have done with the scissors equally, according to the size that you see opening the mouth of the anus, so that the ball makes what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	This instrument is all covered and multiplied in their likenesses; and when the masters have arranged them, the work is more urgent, and higher for humans due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not uncover the instrument unless you have arranged it, as their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her vomit with a mustard poultice, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If it jumps (dislocates) there, it is good.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not (the dislocation does not occur), then take one pot and make a plaster or cup and put in it herbs that can open the mouth of the sore, such as wormwood, rue, anise, chamomile, cascara sagrada and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in water over the fire; then put one end or the cup from the pot into the sore.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	And the pustule until the vapors come within the sore; then make it vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The second sentence to translate:
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and does not heal as expected, command the bailiff to moist his left hand in oil of sulphur or musk oil of altar, and then apply it to nature.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And seek the second incision; and when you have found it, take it and stretch it gently straight, so that the sore does not shrink during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it must be moved gently from right to left, then pull; if you do this, it will come out and dislocate.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	If the mouth of the bladder is stretched, we have said the cure for emptying and the fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it does not have all of what we have said, make sure you do not pull on it.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that the one who is at the mouth of the dead woman, you tie him to the wife's leg, then you clisterize with an ointment four-formula.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	If it will come back and he [the one tied to the wife's leg] will push [the dead woman], but in any case, when she [the dead woman] could come, if it comes badly, it will give off a bad smell at the stomach and head, and sting the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore it is necessary that appropriate fumigations are provided for this case: no ancient has proven the fumigation of parsley and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain the flowers and seconding (afterbirth) is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And has the appearance of glass resembling a canal, and the narrow part is placed in the nature, and the large ends are over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be on the coals, and the time until it is spoiled, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	To pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have their foundations pierced, instead it has been stopped by some subtle means.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary to pierce that substance in its proper place, and do not pierce it with a sharp stylus, and be careful that it does not touch the ligament.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put soft linen soaked in wine and oil on it, then treat with ointment until it heals.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will stay reset, put or insert a splint of wood, and leave it for several days, and let it be removed when the bones appear to have moved in rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes comes this sudden swelling of wound or abscess; it is necessary to cover the sore: if healed, as we have said with a splint of wood.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula at its foundation   (In this context, a fistula is an abnormal passageway or channel between two organs or parts of the body.)
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the foundation are nodulous, and those that come out of it decay faster, or within the space of two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	if there is a fistula or more; and when the nodulous part becomes old, it heals by itself, and in case of moisture wakes up pus or thin boils,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are recognized by those who notice either an excretion or wind when the patient defecates, or in case of accidental passage of gas.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and halfway down the penis; they reach up to the knee joint, and up to the calf of the leg.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes the persistent fistula at its root, but not the non-persistent one:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you press your finger or root on its indication or origin, and insert a fine awl of copper or iron into the fistula when there is no twistedness in it.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	if it has twistedness, then insert a tent or thin strip of linen, or horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair on your finger:
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no purulent discharge, pusor or worms, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not pierce [the skin]; hasten to cure [it].
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is open to the bladder or conducts urine, if it leaks urine and cannot be sealed by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced at the joint of the leg, then the tendon comes to the surface;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no curvature or the location of the pain, it is already bent and does not require medication or salve.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these Persian blisters, there is no cure but work, and the vain efforts of foolish doctors who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In that which is not Persian and not old, for the hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced,
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And let the patient lie between your hands on his back; lift his legs until his thighs are raised to his abdomen, and incline his thighs towards his stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then push a tent of reed, or a plank if there is curvature, until you know where the dislocation comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then you must push your finger as an indicator there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	If you feel then that the tent has pierced it; and if it is discovered where you feel between your finger and the skin or flesh, then you know that it is perforated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work on it, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	Everyone says that some things can be well healed, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that one gives it, is to warm the cautery thinly according to the width of the wound, as previously said;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and put the hot cautery all in the wound, until it comes out of the base; and do this two or three times, as you know that these small charred things should be burned, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then cure the swollen tents with butter, until the inflammation subsides, and then apply a healing ointment, soothing and binding.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it heals in this manner, that is good. But if it cannot be healed otherwise;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it is swollen, do not pierce to the point of the foundation, but between your finger and the swelling, cover with a thick layer of fat or soap, and you will see the fistula beneath the covering.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the end of the fistula begins to swell, push it immediately towards the tent and then apply the fire cautery until it reaches the top of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	The tent will be released and shrink; then burn the charred areas that seem like a feather of a bird, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the flesh is soft and cuts between you and the abscess, cauterize it with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cauterization has two good effects: the burning of the charred areas adjacent to it and the stopping of bleeding and drying of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then treat wounds that are swollen with boiled tentes (a type of cloth) or in a paste made from crushed oats, until the swelling subsides and the charms are burned within the swelling.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with hard charcoal ointments and dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it will be healed and will not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula arises until it reaches the full depth and is located outside of the body, you should press on the affected area or foundation, and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the swelling and it is between two layers or fabrics or leather near the point of piercing, there should be no way out except for a path of faith and hope through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you can cauterize it as we have said, or you can pierce it all the way to the bottom, or if it is pus-filled, you can open and cure it as first mentioned.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep that you cover the substance holding the foundation, and let the purge come out by its own will.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If it will be healed, remove that covering and clean it when it is cut off at the base, either by using a probe or another instrument pointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then remove that charred flesh in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to heal the wound and keep the fistula in the part away from the base, as it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes fistulas are formed in this way: and it is when you push the tent from the fistula, and it is where it adjoins the foundation beneath the skin above,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	Take a lance pierced at the head according to this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	Then push one threaded needle into two, and push the tent all along the thread into the fistula up to the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the margin of the foundation within, then draw out the thread of that one, so that you push your thumb or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And draw the head with thread, and bring together the two shoulders together, and hold one to another, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And do not move it at any time, until the threads tie these characters that are between them have shrunk and closed;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, make it open in all ways that you can, unless it is too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is not advisable to cover a dislocated joint with a plaster, and then cure it while it is still swollen, as we have said, until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spinous spur used to make a fistula is very sharp at one end and sharpened.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and blunt on the other side, because you should not cover what you should not cover, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Emorydes (blisters) are of two types: either they are within the foundation, like a kernel of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in the skin directly blood,
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and there are one or more, and they are swollen away from the foundation and at the head of the foundation; but those which are swollen have less moisture,
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and in the skin or a little citron juice or a little blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the care of those who have it within their foundation, since you instruct the patient to stretch themselves to lie down in chambers, until the foundations heal, and children appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	hasten, and it should be with the pliers, or hold it with your nail, then strike at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the pliers cannot hold it because of moisture, take a small cloth or fabric, or a piece of leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And hold it to your elbows, then strike, and sprinkle powder on top of some hot powders that are in place of fire.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	And you cauterize it as said in the chapter on cautery, then treat other treatments until it is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	If the foundation cannot emerge, then clisterize the patient with biting and sharp clisterium to clean the affected area so that it can come out easily.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient can prevent himself, and if his veins are too deeply pierced, it is a light cure.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grab them with your nail or tweezers and crush them, then heal as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you make the stitch in this way: take one twisted thread, and put it in a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide; draw the thread tightly, then knot the thread, pull out the needle, and do the same with all the others, and leave one for bleeding excess blood.
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a soft cloth soaked in rose oil or pitch on the foundation, and place it on the patient, and instruct him to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then let it drain until it stops, and when it has stopped draining, treat the wound with an ointment and other treatments, until it heals.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	The drying of wounds or foundations.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often, the drying out of wounds occurs in the intestines due to natural constraints and when the disease is old and medicine is of no use.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you cut at the tip of a splint or your nail through the skin above, so as not to let it moisten.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then heal it until it is dry as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot dry, renew the shaving more forcefully than before, until it heals well, and blisters.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then let it heal completely.
dou fremit	The trembling (or shivering)
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A lump (or swelling) is a small protrusion from the body and spreads out greatly.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the throat is frozen (or constricted), and it feels like death by trembling, spreading throughout the entire body, but more so in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the remedy is to take a cane of an ostrich feather or strong goose quill and place it on the trembling, until the purple circles around the trembling completely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand along the entire chain until you grasp it all around the swelling, and immerse it completely, and tighten the swelling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see it (like a chain of iron or steel), do this according to the following form, and be subtle inside and pull it out from above.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce (the swelling), but hold it tightly and press it; and if you see it (the swelling), cauterize it as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of a plaster   \* The text describes how to make a plaster for treating wounds or swellings.\* This sentence is describing the shape that the plaster should have, specifically "the form of a plaster."\* In medieval medical texts, the term "clistere" often refers to a type of ointment or salve used in wound treatment.
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	At times they make a silver or arsenic enema, or molten lead or mercury; and at times they make of these instruments small and large, according to those for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when administering the treatment for children and the weak and sickly, the instruments are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the enema is large or small; it is tied in this manner above, according to this method:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	And there shall be an opening where the belly is joined, as you see, and the head pierced through it; and at one side there should be two holes, and in the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And place the medicines of a beast's bladder or parchment into the opening, and pierce it all around with small holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And have one space between each hole, then put in these holes one strong thread of twisted thread of ten or so, and sew up the belly like a goatskin.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is inside (inside the body), if it is attached to the instrument in front of a strong thread, then plasterize (apply plaster); and this is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the plaster with oil or egg yolk, or similar thing, then press it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the ministers press the plaster with their two hands together until it is completely flat, then remove the plaster, and make the patient spread his legs apart.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if you want the medicine to work, stretch it as much as possible; and if it swells up for an entire night, it will be of greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you want to treat a disease of abdominal distention, and the medicine works quickly, repeat it until it becomes healthy.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are foundation or abscess, the clyster should be as subtle as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the form of the subtle cluster on top of which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have said in the previous section the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you about the care for hands and medicines, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to what they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of how they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by piercing with a spear, cutting with a sword and knife, or of a lance or fist or arrow, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the parts of the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, head, chest, abdomen, liver and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with wounds on the head, for it will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	If a simple wound comes on the head and the bone is not broken, then take care if it is due to an arrow or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large.
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	And if you doubt the rise of an abscess hot: let it heal itself from the head itself immediately, even if a little blood comes from the wound, and it should heal in the opposite direction of the infected part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And the patient should empty himself of wine and thick foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	If he does not want to urinate, let his food be reduced, and he should not drink wine, nor eat meat;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And put on the wound, if an abscess comes, only soft wool soaked in rose oil or in stiptic wine.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no abscess hot, put it on the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood, and it is not moving due to air or powder, I will say a little more about this later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has moved [infected], put some medicinal herbs on it until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like the size of a sword and of similar appearance, and the lips cannot be brought together by pressing, then join them with stitches, as I will explain for abdominal wounds, through stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed of the bone and gaping, and does not hold but only a little, close it; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Instruct the patient to eat thick foods such as cooked heads and wheat, also pulses, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or suspect putrid flesh not on the bone, close it all and throw it away, then treat it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein that cannot be stopped without cutting it off, and it does not stop bleeding with medicine, then cut the artery, and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	If it does not help, cauterize (it).
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if the wounds are small and simple, it is an easy cure: and it is that you put this powder which cements them once the herb has moved (it).
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of the powder is as follows: take incense one part, dragon's blood 2 parts, quicklime 4 parts, and grind it finely.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And apply the wound, pressing it until it exudes well and merges with all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then tie it well and leave it to heal if it does not swell; because the medicine is not removed until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	Sometimes this is done only with chalk, when no incense or dragon's blood is available, but the wound has not moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	If the wound has moved, it should not be used in this case, do not apply this powder.
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	But apply some digestive herbs, or barley flour boiled in water and honey until it thickens.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	If a bone breakage comes with the wound and it is small, extract it with subtle tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you after the fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	Of the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound comes in or on the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between that and one on the head, but if the nerve of the neck or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is no other remedy than to leave it to heal and not put anything binding, for it harms the nerve and causes it to retreat;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and not to put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but the medicine should be like salt washed in soft water and mixed with rose oil, and boiled also in soft water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of a similar kind, moistened.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, wrap it with bandages, then treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and swollen with pus, pierce it or lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the arteries are cut and bleeding occurs, tie it off, ligate it, and cauterize as needed.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the spine of the throat is cut or the windpipe is damaged, keep the airway protected, so that food goes.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If the swelling is on the neck above the throat, do not touch the throat but reset it according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then allow it to come down and wait for some days, then treat with burning ointments until it is healed.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	If the wound presses into the bone, cut it open.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	If there are bone fragments, remove them all if you can, and leave those that cannot be removed until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let the dislocation be separated and aligned.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	If the wound is fresh, sprinkle the powder that I have said on it.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound caused by lance or knife.   --> of the lance or knife wound
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's a wound from a lance or knife, and the wound is deep, look if vapors rise from the wound as the patient breathes; therefore know that the wound is fatal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and it is fresh with all its blood, do not apply powder at first hour nor tie it for the blood that dissolves it.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the patient's heart, and cut off the wound.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	But you apply an attractive ointment, and let it rest twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you do not have ointment, put old cotton on the wound to draw out moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm, nor bad tremors of the heart, or training of a dog does not occur.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see good positions, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then from cuts and other remedies, as long as he is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot heal and open, then know that there is a fistula; treat it as necessary.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword cut or a knife, and it is simple, or deeper, or on the back, treat that which is in front of it;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, stitch it up; if it is small, apply powder to it; if it has pierced the bone and broken into fragments, whichever the wound, and the veins are exposed, pull them back if they are protruding.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not exposed, let the wound drain, align the extraction;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	the dislocation of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The dislocation of the belly can be great and medium-sized or small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, at times the intestines themselves may protrude, or the nerves of the intestines, by which they cannot be inserted.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worth more than a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because when replacing the intestines, more points are needed if they are not placed one by one;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell quickly and feel the cold, so they enter with more points,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and because the middle wound is more important, for this reason, stitch the intestines back in their place instead of using two (points) like others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the ruptures of the belly are according to four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common types occur in the abdominal hernia,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the hernias of other body parts and two other specific hernias occur in other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all of them are more suitable with the stitching of the stomach, and I will say each one and explain it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	When the wound is small, and nothing from the intestines protrudes out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and there are two ways to set it (the bone), here is the first one:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	for the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	for because the intestines are swollen due to the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	soak a sponge or one piece of linen cloth only in hot water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	Or you cook in sharp quince and cypress and spike,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and open the intestines as long as the inflammation is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes make this wine restraining, and it is said to be effective for reducing swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the inflammation disappearing, if the intestines are cooked in water that is too hot or spoiled,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	For this purpose, the entry is closed tightly.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, then make a small opening in the wound with an instrument used to treat hemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is made from crushed boiled peas.
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	We should not cut it without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument for cutting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	Cut into the hollow part but not through, and observe the shape.
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the internal parts protrude outward,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	Put it back in its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you have the power to do so, for it is necessary.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and located in the area beneath the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you must make the patient lie down on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and raise their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	And if it is in the part beneath the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	hold the head and foot higher than the parts below.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	hold your intention that the injured part should be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus the treatment should be administered as I say for large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds apply what is appropriate.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have a compassionate minister between your hands who anoints the entire wound with his hand.
et assemble les levres;	and press the lips together.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common method of suturing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take one needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave from the head of the wound two fingers' width, and sew with a needle that has one strong thread.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two skin layers with the two knives (or small blades).
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	Who is beneath the skin within, as long as you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and assemble the two heads of the scaphoid (the small finger bone) in four groups.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then bind with a double thread around the needle of two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then assemble the two heads of the wound facing each other,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave one hole's space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	and tie the thread as you did with the first needle.
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing so according to what you need for the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the whole wound is bound up;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And let the needles be medium sized, neither too thin nor thick.
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	For the fine needles pierce through the whole skin, and the thick ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they should be medium sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to insert needles too deeply into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not split and open the wound before the bond.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then put the points of the needles in, so that they do not prick the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and put cloth or bandages on the tips of the needles to keep them in place,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	And leave [the wound] until it heals.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this stitching method with needles is more suitable for small wounds.
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it pierces an awl or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitching is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it is that you gather together the two shoulders of skin and the two shoulders of flesh together with a needle where there is one strong, medium thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced these four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	if you remove the needle from the part where you began, in the manner that one sews garments;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And place a space between each stitch the size of a small egg.
ceste costure sevent li home,	This stitching shall be for the man.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound on one side or abdomen of a person,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was wounded by a knife.
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	And the wound was more than one palm wide,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	And the intestines were about two palms wide.
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	The wound was in the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine after it had been out for twenty-four hours,
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound was sewn up for fifteen days, it healed, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, but it was a miracle.
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not cure him with ointment, for I was in one place where there was none to be found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I put old cotton over the wound twice a day, and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	And I will tell you the two proper ways of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and poke it from the outside part through to within that.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has pierced the core straight through straight, lay the skin or fabric over where you inserted the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make it pierce from the inside part to the outside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And the understanding of this stitch is that you sew it as a pelter makes fur.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave a space once on one side, and return it from the other, until the stitch is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second manner of stitching, which Galen himself calls,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is so that anyone who assembles the two parts together naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And press one of the shoulders against the other shoulder, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	thrust an awl or the shoulder of the mirror-side into that spot only,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	leave the two shoulders of the face;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the awl, and pierce it from the outside part to that inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	2 shoulder bones
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then make a hole in one and the other from the outer part until within, in 2 other shoulder bones that are on the opposite side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the manner of stitching and the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one denies it.
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must sew the belly with two needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one must thrust one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew leather.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	And know that when the incision is inside the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The stitching is more painful than other parts of the stomach.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments of the wound are like the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you probe the fresh wound with all its blood, as soon as the arrow has moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if you replace the intestines and tie it up; then place powdered scented char on top of it.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	And if the elbow has moved, put any available ointment on it until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And tie up the thread, and bind the suture, and apply the mire.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then heal the wound as with others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you don't have medicine, put old cotton on it as soon as it starts to heal;
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And move it two times a day as long as it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you have no need for other medicines in many cases where the wounds are simple.
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt whether the wound causes communion with the main parts,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you moisten linen lightly with heated oil, or rose oil.
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the sores, and under the saddle(like a bandage);
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if there is pain or putrefaction in the belly, and this occurs repeatedly,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If the black vinegar enemas become cold, and especially if putrefaction reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within, know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The "jeun" intestine cannot heal when perforated.
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is due to the pus in the veins that are there, and the subtlety of the whole body, and the proximity of its nature to the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the worm jumps from the wound, put it back as the intestine, while it is still fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and turned black, then you should cut the black part, so that blood does not flow from there.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	for there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then cut what is between the ligament;
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and hang the two heads suspended from the part below the wound so as to align the extraction when the bladder falls out, and the wound opens.
de la routure dou boueil	Of the rupture of the eyeball
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	it can be restored in some people,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I saw a man pierced or stabbed in the stomach;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	The wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and became abscessed and turned into a fistula, with discharge and flatulence.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it according to what I knew, and continued to cauterize until it healed, and the flesh closed over.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw the flesh heal, I feared that the patient might have an illness in his abdomen;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	And it had no ill, but improved in better conditions, and ate and drank.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and said some experienced people that when it has a small wound in the intestine, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large thread, then gather the lips of the wound.
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the thread has gone through the mouth, place it on the two lips.
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if she pulls her mouth up;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then he strikes the head, and hold him so that he cannot dislocate.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then place another blow in this manner until the wound is completely seized;
et cout la plaie.	and cauterize the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	The first sentence translates to: If the head is swollen in the intestines, it causes no harm to the patient.
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	and a thin thread can be tied around the intestine that is cut from an animal's intestine.
en teil maniere:	in this way:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the head (of the thread) made from intestine, which should be very sharp.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then tie this thread to the head of the linen cord (or very thin linen thread).
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then thread the needle and sew the intestine, and pull it through the opening.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching the wound is not beyond the way of faith and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the great intestines, there is no remedy or health, except for subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from fistula or that it is
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it grows old, is universally called "fistula".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and especially when it becomes large and swollen.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the truth a hard and white nodulation where there is no pain.
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is as hollow as the feather of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	sometimes it clears up quickly, and other times it remains thick.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes small, and other times quite;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken of it in the section on wounds, that every wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	this is not further than by one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	it means, through the littleness of the blood or body:
ou por sa malice;	or by its malice;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	And because there is hard flesh within, and above the lips, do not let it produce any more flesh.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	And there is too much pus.
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	The limb is rotten, and the matter is of bad quality.
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	The medicine is not good in the treatment.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	For because corruption is a kind of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	for in the property of the region, digestion is slow and health sluggish, and it tends to run down by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	there are veins or bones;
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, the signs, and the treatments of medicines in the section on diseases.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Now I will tell you how to treat a fistula that is made by handwork.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or to the small intestine, or to the bladder, or to one of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or to the spine of the back, or to any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if such a thing comes to the property of the main member, and similar lesser members.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are of this kind are difficult to heal, except with labor, and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	but if there is any fistula that does not come up to the level I have said, and you have faith in its cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	and you observe it, if it is straight, take a tent of beeswax or iron, if the fistula is straight, insert it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is twisted, look for a thin reed tent,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	For the plough bends towards tortuosity.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula is severely damaged and you cannot find it by probing,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	If you cleanse one of the wounds,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	Because moisture spreads from one wound to another, and it cleanses.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then pierce it cauterously in your power, knowing if there is bone or nerve, and if it is completely healed.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when you press your hand, and where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know the place where it is, and if it is far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery or a vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the places I have told you, if the head follows according to what I have said,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and remove the falsehood and rotten matter that is within it;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then heal it until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is well penetrated straight through, it is necessary that you cauterize thoroughly, as much as you can.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then apply dampened plugs soaked in hot medicine to the base of the fistula.
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine dissolves the excess matter that remains at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then apply clean oil to it, as long as it is pure.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if it is not healthy by this means, then cauterize as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is corrupted due to the fistula, cut (it).
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerve does not obstruct or affect major limbs as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed and there is corruption and blackness, scrape off all the corruption as much as possible.
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the harmful things while he is healthy;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if he is not healthy, bend it as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you are not going until the font;
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	dig deep and seek as far as you are able,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	And remove all corruption, then reset the place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, that is well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too deep, that you cannot reach it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	If there is no other instrument but the ligature from nature;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small bone corrupted, and you can draw it with the pliers,
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if it should be pulled out with one instrument,
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, pull them all out, leave none.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	And if moisture opposes it and there is no error or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	And if the flesh covers and holds together the bones,
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, put something healing and purifying on the wound.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it heal until the flesh grows around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And then if they have the bones more lightly;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	If it is a large bone, like in the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	if only remove the corruption until the blackness is completely removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	Then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is great corruption in it, reaching down to the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	it must be cut off and covered all the way up to the corruption, and then it should be cured until it heals.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	I will tell you about a fistula that happened to a man in his leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	If you take an example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was once a young man of about thirty years old who had pain in his leg due to something coming from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	The matter came to the leg, and a large abscess formed which could not be opened by any other means;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but the masters, out of their folly, opened the abscess too much,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	And it becomes extremely rotten with matter, and a fistula forms, and much pus comes out that all are going with moisture from the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and they put many remedies in it for two years, and no wise man had knowledge of cures by hand.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	until I was summoned there, and saw the leg and the medicines they were using to treat it.
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and he who runs through the wounds with great speed;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and the heart of the young man turns red, and has a yellow complexion.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent at one of the wounds, then searched for all the wounds,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and I found that one wound came from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I therefore hastened and made an incision in one of the sores until I discovered a part of the bone.
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and found it corrupted and pierced through, and the corruption went to the bone inside;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I was of the opinion that there was no other corruption in the bone, except what I left behind.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and I began to treat the wound with salves for a long time, but could not heal it;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	And then examine, uncover the bone as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	and find the continuous corruption in the bone, cut it out, then leave it open and I will try to heal the place.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I was not able to cut more than a palm of the bone around it, and let it hang by the muscle all over.
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	then I restored it with medicine; and it healed and grew strong quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	And it is not necessary to start work again except due to the weakness of the patient, who cannot endure.
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and due to the fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For it frequently evacuated blood, but he was healed entirely,
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And a hard cartilage was born in its place instead of the bone, and it had a good arrangement and no harm or contrary effects at all, neither to the air nor to the future.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken anywhere in the body, it must be set in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	take a splint and bind it to the open end of the broken bone,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	command anyone who can to extend the limb upward;
